[grid-area:main] px-4 py-6 gap-4 md:px-6 md:pt-8 xl:px-8 xl:pt-14 *:max-w-225"><div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground"><span class="truncate text-fd-primary font-medium">Overview</span></div><div class="flex flex-col md:flex-row items-start gap-4 pt-2 pb-1 md:justify-between"><h1 class="text-[1.75em] font-semibold">Overview of Prisma Schema</h1><div class="flex flex-row gap-2 items-center"><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring border bg-fd-secondary text-fd-secondary-foreground hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-base-ui-click-trigger="" id="base-ui-_R_3sculubv5ubv9db_" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring border bg-fd-secondary text-fd-secondary-foreground hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground px-2 py-1.5 text-xs gap-2">Open<i class="fa-regular fa-chevron-down text-[0.875rem] text-fd-muted-foreground"></i></button></div></div><p class="mb-2 text-lg text-fd-muted-foreground">The Prisma schema is the main method of configuration when using Prisma. It is typically called schema.prisma and contains your database connection and data model</p><div class="prose flex-1"><p>The Prisma Schema (or <em>schema</em> for short) is the main method of configuration for your Prisma ORM setup. It consists of the following parts:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/overview/data-sources"><strong>Data sources</strong></a>: Specify the details of the data sources Prisma ORM should connect to (e.g. a PostgreSQL database)</li>
<li><a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/overview/generators"><strong>Generators</strong></a>: Specifies what clients should be generated based on the data model (e.g. Prisma Client)</li>
<li><a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/data-model/models"><strong>Data model definition</strong></a>: Specifies your application <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/data-model/models#defining-models">models</a> (the shape of the data per data source) and their <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/data-model/relations">relations</a></li>
</ul>
<p>It is typically a single file called <code>schema.prisma</code> (or multiple files with <code>.prisma</code> file extension) that is stored in a defined but customizable <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/overview/location">location</a>. You can also <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/overview/location#multi-file-prisma-schema">organize your Prisma schema in multiple files</a> if you prefer that.</p>
<p>See the <a href="/docs/orm/reference/prisma-schema-reference">Prisma schema API reference</a> <span class="api"></span> for detailed information about each section of the schema.</p>
<p>Whenever a <code>prisma</code> command is invoked, the CLI typically reads some information from the schema, e.g.:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>prisma generate</code>: Reads <em>all</em> above mentioned information from the Prisma schema to generate the correct data source client code (e.g. Prisma Client).</li>
<li><code>prisma migrate dev</code>: Reads the data sources and data model definition to create a new migration.</li>
</ul>
<p>You can also <a href="#accessing-environment-variables-from-the-schema">use environment variables</a> inside the schema to provide configuration options when a CLI command is invoked.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="example"><a data-card="" href="#example" class="peer">Example</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The following is an example of a Prisma Schema that specifies:</p>
<ul>
<li>A data source (PostgreSQL or MongoDB)</li>
<li>A generator (Prisma Client)</li>
<li>A data model definition with two models (with one relation) and one <code>enum</code></li>
<li>Several <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/data-model/models#native-types-mapping">native data type attributes</a> (<code>@db.VarChar(255)</code>, <code>@db.ObjectId</code>)</li>
</ul>
<div dir="ltr" data-orientation="horizontal" class="bg-background-default rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral overflow-hidden my-4"><div role="tablist" aria-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-row px-2 overflow-x-auto text-fd-muted-foreground bg-background-default" tabindex="-1" data-orientation="horizontal" style="outline:none"><div class="flex items-center bottom-0 h-px group-data-[state=active]:bg-fd-primary"></div>Relational Databases</button><button type="button" role="tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="radix-_R_1asulubv5ubv9db_-content-MongoDB" data-state="inactive" id="radix-_R_1asulubv5ubv9db_-trigger-MongoDB" class="relative group inline-flex type-text-sm-strong text-nowrap data-radix-collection-item=""><div class="absolute inset-x-2 bottom-0 h-px group-data-[state=active]:bg-fd-primary"></div>MongoDB</button></div></div><div data-state="active" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  role      </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Role</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">     @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">USER</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  posts     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Post</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">[]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Post</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">      @id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">autoincrement</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  createdAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">now</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  updatedAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @updatedAt</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  published </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Boolean</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">false</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">255</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  author    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">     @relation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">fields</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">authorId</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">references</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  authorId  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">enum</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Role</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  USER</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_1asulubv5ubv9db_-trigger-MongoDB" hidden="" id="radix-_R_1asulubv5ubv9db_-content-MongoDB" tabindex="0"></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="syntax"><a data-card="" href="#syntax" class="peer">Syntax</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Prisma Schema files are written in Prisma Schema Language (PSL). See the <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/overview/data-sources">data sources</a>, <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/overview/generators">generators</a>, <a href="/docs/orm/prisma-schema/data-model/models">data model definition</a> and of course <a href="/docs/orm/reference/prisma-schema-reference">Prisma Schema API reference</a> pages for details and examples.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="vs-code"><a data-card="" href="#vs-code" class="peer">VS Code</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Syntax highlighting for PSL is available via a <a href="https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=Prisma.prisma" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">VS Code extension</a> (which also lets you auto-format the contents of your Prisma schema and indicates syntax errors with red squiggly lines). Learn more about <a href="/docs/orm/more/dev-environment/editor-setup">setting up Prisma ORM in your editor</a>.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="github"><a data-card="" href="#github" class="peer">GitHub</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>PSL code snippets on GitHub can be rendered with syntax highlighting as well by using the <code>.prisma</code> file extension or annotating fenced code blocks in Markdown with <code>prisma</code>:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">```</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model User {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        Int      @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  createdAt DateTime @default(now())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email     String   @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name      String?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">```</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="accessing-environment-variables-from-the-schema"><a data-card="" href="#accessing-environment-variables-from-the-schema" class="peer">Accessing environment variables from the schema</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>You can use environment variables to provide configuration options when a CLI command is invoked, or a Prisma Client query is run.</p>
<p>Hardcoding URLs directly in your schema is possible but is discouraged because it poses a security risk. Using environment variables in the schema allows you to <strong>keep secrets out of the schema</strong> which in turn <strong>improves the portability of the schema</strong> by allowing you to use it in different environments.</p>
<p>Environment variables can be accessed using the <code>env()</code> function:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">datasource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> db</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>You can use the <code>env()</code> function in the following places:</p>
<ul>
<li>A datasource url</li>
<li>Generator binary targets</li>
</ul>
<p>See <a href="/docs/orm/more/dev-environment/environment-variables">Environment variables</a> for more information about how to use an <code>.env</code> file during development.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="comments"><a data-card="" href="#comments" class="peer">Comments</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>There are three types of comments that are supported in Prisma Schema Language:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>// comment</code>: This comment is for the reader&#x27;s clarity and is not present in the abstract syntax tree (AST) of the schema.</li>
<li><code>/// comment</code>: These comments will show up in the abstract syntax tree (AST) of the schema as descriptions to AST nodes. Tools can then use these comments to provide additional information. All comments are attached to the next available node - <a href="https://github.com/prisma/prisma/issues/3544" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">free-floating comments</a> are not supported and are not included in the AST.</li>
<li><code>/* block comment */</code>: These comments will show up in the abstract syntax tree, similarly to <code>///</code> comments.</li>
</ul>
<p>Here are some different examples:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">/// This comment will get attached to the `User` node in the AST</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  /// This comment will get attached to the `id` node in the AST</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">autoincrement</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // This comment is just for you</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  weight </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"> /// This comment gets attached to the `weight` node</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// This comment is just for you. It will not</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// show up in the AST.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">/// This comment will get attached to the</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">/// Customer node.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Customer</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  /**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">   * ...and so will this comment</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">   */</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="auto-formatting"><a data-card="" href="#auto-formatting" class="peer">Auto formatting</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Prisma ORM supports formatting <code>.prisma</code> files automatically. There are two ways to format <code>.prisma</code> files:</p>
<ul>
<li>Run the <a href="/docs/orm/reference/prisma-cli-reference#format"><code>prisma format</code></a> <span class="api"></span> command.</li>
<li>Install the <a href="https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=Prisma.prisma" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Prisma VS Code extension</a> and invoke the <a href="https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/codebasics#_formatting" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">VS Code format action</a> - manually or on save.</li>
</ul>
<p>There are no configuration options - <a href="#formatting-rules">formatting rules</a> are fixed (similar to Golang&#x27;s <code>gofmt</code> but unlike Javascript&#x27;s <code>prettier</code>):</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="formatting-rules"><a data-card="" href="#formatting-rules" class="peer">Formatting rules</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="configuration-blocks-are-aligned-by-theirsign"><a data-card="" href="#configuration-blocks-are-aligned-by-theirsign" class="peer">Configuration blocks are aligned by their = sign</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>block _ {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  key      = &quot;value&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  key2     = 1</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  long_key = true</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="field-definitions-are-aligned-into-columns-separated-by-2-or-more-spaces"><a data-card="" href="#field-definitions-are-aligned-into-columns-separated-by-2-or-more-spaces" class="peer">Field definitions are aligned into columns separated by 2 or more spaces</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>block _ {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  id          String       @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  first_name  LongNumeric  @default</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="empty-lines-resets-block-alignment-and-formatting-rules"><a data-card="" href="#empty-lines-resets-block-alignment-and-formatting-rules" class="peer">Empty lines resets block alignment and formatting rules</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>block _ {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span>  key10 = true</span></span>

<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>block _ {</span></span>

<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="multiline-field-attributes-are-properly-aligned-with-the-rest-of-the-field-attributes"><a data-card="" href="#multiline-field-attributes-are-properly-aligned-with-the-rest-of-the-field-attributes" class="peer">Multiline field attributes are properly aligned with the rest of the field attributes</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>block _ {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span>}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="block-attributes-are-sorted-to-the-end-of-the-block"><a data-card="" href="#block-attributes-are-sorted-to-the-end-of-the-block" class="peer">Block attributes are sorted to the end of the block</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden type-code-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>block _ {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  key   = &quot;value&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  @@attribute</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure></div><div class="flex flex-row flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4 border-t pt-6 text-sm"><a target="_blank"
